---
about_this_resource_text: "<p><strong>Description:</strong> What can be inferred about\
  \ a graph from its second eigenvalue? Professor Zhao explores the role of spectra\
  \ in pseudorandom graphs. Some topics discussed are Payley graphs and Gauss sums,\
  \ quasirandom Cayley graphs, and the Alon\u2013Boppana bound.\r\n\r\n</p>\r\n<p><strong>Instructor:</strong>\
  \ Yufei Zhao</p>"
course_id: 18-217-graph-theory-and-additive-combinatorics-fall-2019

  <span m="292790">group</span> <span m="293900">and</span> <span m="294180">the</span>
  <span m="294320">set</span> <span m="294830">S</span> <span m="295580">to</span>
  <span m="295730">be</span> <span m="295880">the</span> <span m="295970">following</span>
  <span m="296480">graph,</span> <span m="301400">where</span> <span m="302290">V,</span>
  <span m="302920">the</span> <span m="303020">set</span> <span m="303290">of</span>
  <span m="303530">vertices,</span> <span m="304160">is</span> <span m="304370">just</span>
  <span m="304790">the</span> <span m="305180">set</span> <span m="305450">of</span>
  <span m="305600">group</span> <span m="306080">elements.</span> <span m="307190">And</span>
  <span m="307430">the</span> <span m="307610">edges</span> <span m="310750">are</span>
  <span m="313120">obtained</span> <span m="314050">by</span> <span m="314500">taking</span>
  <span m="315200">a</span> <span m="315310">group</span> <span m="315580">element</span>
  <span m="316240">and</span> <span m="316630">multiplying</span> <span m="317230">it</span>
  <span m="317320">by</span> <span m="317560">S</span> <span m="318530">to</span>
  <span m="318820">go</span> <span m="319000">to</span> <span m="319720">its</span>
  <span m="319990">neighbor.</span> <span m="326480">So</span> <span m="326530">this</span>
  <span m="326710">is</span> <span m="326800">a</span> <span m="326860">Cayley</span>
  <span m="327115">graph.</span> <span m="328030">And</span> <span m="328660">Cayley</span>
  <span m="328990">graphs</span> <span m="329470">are--</span> <span m="330670">start</span>
  <span m="330970">with</span> <span m="331150">any</span> <span m="331360">group,</span>
  <span m="331600">start</span> <span m="331840">with</span> <span m="331990">any</span>
  <span m="332140">subset</span> <span m="332830">of</span> <span m="332920">the</span>
  <span m="333010">group,</span> <span m="333380">you</span> <span m="333480">get</span>
  <span m="333550">a</span> <span m="333610">Cayley</span> <span m="333880">graph.</span>
  <span m="334120">And</span> <span m="334210">this</span> <span m="334360">is</span>
  <span m="334510">a</span> <span m="334960">very</span> <span m="335170">important</span>
  <span m="335560">construction</span> <span m="336570">of</span> <span m="336700">graphs.</span>
  <span m="337260">They</span> <span m="337360">have</span> <span m="337810">lots</span>
  <span m="338020">of</span> <span m="338110">nice</span> <span m="338350">properties</span></p><p><span
  m="339630">And,</span> <span m="340030">in</span> <span m="340150">particular,</span>
  <span m="341790">an</span> <span m="342040">example</span> <span m="342490">of</span>
  <span m="342580">a</span> <span m="342610">Cayley</span> <span m="342940">graph</span>
  <span m="344230">is</span> <span m="344950">a</span> <span m="345010">Paley</span>
  <span m="345400">graph.</span> <span m="349830">They're</span> <span m="350090">not</span>
  <span m="350240">related.</span> <span m="351750">So</span> <span m="352180">a</span>
  <span m="352220">Paley</span> <span m="352610">graph</span> <span m="353420">is</span>
  <span m="353810">a</span> <span m="353930">special</span> <span m="354380">case</span>
  <span m="354650">of</span> <span m="354740">a</span> <span m="354800">Cayley</span>
  <span m="355100">graph</span> <span m="356000">obtained</span> <span m="356630">by</span>
  <span m="358070">considering</span> <span m="360260">the</span> <span m="360380">group,</span>
  <span m="361990">the</span> <span m="362130">cyclic</span> <span m="362490">group</span>
  <span m="363440">mod</span> <span m="363830">p,</span> <span m="364490">where</span>
  <span m="364670">p</span> <span m="366620">is</span> <span m="367610">prime</span>
  <span m="367895">1</span> <span m="368180">mod</span> <span m="368360">4.</span>
  <span m="372110">And</span> <span m="372650">I'm</span> <span m="372830">looking</span>
  <span m="373190">at</span> <span m="373370">S</span> <span m="374978">being</span>
  <span m="375380">the</span> <span m="375500">set</span> <span m="375770">of</span>
  <span m="376070">quadratic</span> <span m="376640">residues,</span> <span m="377080">mod</span>
  <span m="377450">p.</span> <span m="384810">It's</span> <span m="385070">actually</span>
  <span m="385310">nonzero</span> <span m="386210">quadratic</span> <span m="386690">residues.</span>
  <span m="388580">So</span> <span m="389330">elements</span> <span m="389690">of</span>
  <span m="389780">mod</span> <span m="389960">p</span> <span m="390170">that</span>
  <span m="390320">could</span> <span m="390500">be</span> <span m="391150">a</span>
  <span m="391300">square.</span></p><p><span m="393970">So</span> <span m="395280">we</span>
  <span m="395460">will</span> <span m="395610">show</span> <span m="395850">in</span>
  <span m="395970">a</span> <span m="396000">second</span> <span m="396480">that</span>

  <span m="590340">them.</span> <span m="599510">So</span> <span m="599640">these</span>

  <span m="617200">the</span> <span m="617320">other</span> <span m="617530">ones,</span>
  <span m="618060">we'll</span> <span m="618190">just</span> <span m="618340">do</span>
  <span m="618490">this</span> <span m="618640">computation.</span> <span m="622860">So</span>
  <span m="623080">instead</span> <span m="623440">of</span> <span m="624250">getting</span>
  <span m="624490">confused</span> <span m="624910">with</span> <span m="625060">indices,</span>
  <span m="625570">let</span> <span m="625690">me</span> <span m="626350">just</span>
  <span m="626620">compute,</span> <span m="627250">as</span> <span m="627400">an</span>
  <span m="627460">example,</span> <span m="628000">the</span> <span m="628390">j-th</span>
  <span m="629200">coordinate</span> <span m="631110">of</span> <span m="632340">the</span>
  <span m="633560">adjacency</span> <span m="633780">matrix</span> <span m="634500">times</span>
  <span m="635260">V2.</span> <span m="637712">So</span> <span m="638200">the</span>
  <span m="638370">j-th</span> <span m="638650">coordinate,</span> <span m="639180">so</span>

  <span m="639990">to,</span> <span m="642360">is</span> <span m="644280">the</span>
  <span m="644370">following</span> <span m="644820">sum.</span> <span m="645630">If</span>
  <span m="645750">I</span> <span m="645880">run</span> <span m="646200">over</span>
  <span m="646540">S,</span> <span m="648160">then</span> <span m="648890">omega</span>
  <span m="649580">raised</span> <span m="649910">to</span> <span m="650540">j</span>
  <span m="651170">plus</span> <span m="651680">s.</span> <span m="652110">So</span>
  <span m="652370">S</span> <span m="652740">is</span> <span m="653630">symmetric,</span>
  <span m="654260">so</span> <span m="654380">I</span> <span m="654440">don't</span>
  <span m="654590">have</span> <span m="654680">to</span> <span m="654800">worry</span>

  <span m="657080">So</span> <span m="657560">I</span> <span m="657590">say</span>

  <span m="659870">this</span> <span m="660040">Cayley</span> <span m="660490">graph,</span>
  <span m="660740">how</span> <span m="660920">it</span> <span m="661020">is</span>

  <span m="860180">consider</span> <span m="861110">the</span> <span m="861200">square</span>

  <span m="899260">expanding.</span> <span m="901390">But</span> <span m="901540">now</span>
  <span m="903790">you</span> <span m="903880">see,</span> <span m="904060">if</span>

  <span m="917060">algebra.</span></p><p><span m="918350">And</span> <span m="918380">now</span>
  <span m="918710">you</span> <span m="918830">notice</span> <span m="919250">that</span>
  <span m="919880">this</span> <span m="920420">sum</span> <span m="920900">here,</span>

  <span m="933250">claim</span> <span m="933640">that</span> <span m="935930">this</span>
  <span m="936080">sum</span> <span m="936380">is</span> <span m="936470">0.</span>
  <span m="936850">And</span> <span m="937100">when</span> <span m="937380">b is</span>
  <span m="937750">nonzero,</span> <span m="938620">then</span> <span m="938920">I'm</span>
  <span m="939200">summing</span> <span m="939620">over</span> <span m="939890">some</span>

  <span m="943910">So</span> <span m="944410">here</span> <span m="944620">I'm</span>

  <span m="952080">So</span> <span m="952270">I'm</span> <span m="952560">re-parameterizing</span>
  <span m="953500">k</span> <span m="953770">a</span> <span m="953830">little</span>
  <span m="954040">bit.</span> <span m="954445">So</span> <span m="954700">k</span>

  <span m="956020">Then</span> <span m="956410">when</span> <span m="956590">b</span>

  <span m="960310">it equals</span> <span m="960730">to</span> <span m="960850">p.</span>
  <span m="961720">So</span> <span m="962590">the</span> <span m="962770">sum</span>

  <span m="964990">to</span> <span m="965640">p.</span></p><p><span m="969090">And,</span>
  <span m="969210">therefore,</span> <span m="971430">lambda</span> <span m="971790">k,</span>
  <span m="972450">lambda sub k--</span> <span m="977520">how</span> <span m="977730">about</span>
  <span m="978180">if</span> <span m="978540">I--</span> <span m="980270">so</span>
  <span m="980910">what</span> <span m="981070">should</span> <span m="981270">I</span>

  <span m="1300180">a</span> <span m="1300280">large--</span> <span m="1300950">so</span>

  <span m="1301970">regular</span> <span m="1302360">graph.</span> <span m="1302710">So</span>
  <span m="1302810">let's</span> <span m="1302990">say</span> <span m="1303240">a</span>
  <span m="1303340">large</span> <span m="1304820">random</span> <span m="1305300">d</span>
  <span m="1305760">regular</span> <span m="1305900">graph.</span> <span m="1310164">d</span>
  <span m="1310660">here</span> <span m="1310930">can</span> <span m="1311080">be</span>
  <span m="1311170">a</span> <span m="1311230">constant</span> <span m="1311860">or</span>
  <span m="1312580">growing</span> <span m="1313000">with n,</span> <span m="1313390">but</span>
  <span m="1313570">this is a</span> <span m="1313930">pretty</span> <span m="1314200">robust</span>
  <span m="1314740">example.</span> <span m="1315670">And</span> <span m="1315790">then</span>
  <span m="1316060">I</span> <span m="1316330">add</span> <span m="1316510">to</span>
  <span m="1316780">it</span> <span m="1318190">an</span> <span m="1318400">extra</span>
  <span m="1319120">destroying</span> <span m="1319630">copy</span> <span m="1320050">of</span>
  <span m="1320230">k sub d plus 1</span> <span m="1322480">that's</span> <span m="1322690">much</span>
  <span m="1322930">smaller</span> <span m="1323830">in</span> <span m="1323950">terms</span>

  <span m="1324640">vertices.</span></p><p><span m="1327500">The</span> <span m="1327620">big,</span>

  <span m="1347390">just</span> <span m="1347570">adding</span> <span m="1347840">a</span>

  <span m="1373810">that</span> <span m="1373960">graph.</span> <span m="1375120">These</span>

  <span m="1421190">because,</span> <span m="1422210">if</span> <span m="1422300">you</span>

  <span m="1428610">Cayley</span> <span m="1428870">graph--</span> <span m="1429260">for--</span>
  <span m="1430700">if</span> <span m="1430820">you</span> <span m="1430940">have</span>
  <span m="1431360">the</span> <span m="1431480">eigenvalue</span> <span m="1431990">condition,</span>

  <span m="1438520">most</span> <span m="1438950">n.</span> <span m="1442520">So</span>
  <span m="1443150">if</span> <span m="1444520">lambda</span> <span m="1446000">is</span>
  <span m="1446540">quite</span> <span m="1446840">small</span> <span m="1448260">compared</span>

  <span m="1453180">type</span> <span m="1453420">of</span> <span m="1453590">quasi-randomness.</span>
  <span m="1456030">So</span> <span m="1456180">I'll</span> <span m="1456270">make</span>
  <span m="1456480">the</span> <span m="1456570">statements</span> <span m="1456960">more</span>
  <span m="1457200">precise</span> <span m="1457620">in</span> <span m="1457710">a</span>
  <span m="1457770">second.</span></p><p><span m="1461420">So</span> <span m="1461540">the</span>
  <span m="1461610">question</span> <span m="1461880">is,</span> <span m="1462100">how</span>
  <span m="1462390">can</span> <span m="1462600">we</span> <span m="1463230">certify,</span>

  <span m="1466560">fact,</span> <span m="1466980">DISC,</span> <span m="1468090">which</span>
  <span m="1468300">is</span> <span m="1468540">seemingly</span> <span m="1469050">weaker</span>

  <span m="1470550">stronger</span> <span m="1470940">property</span> <span m="1471370">of</span>
  <span m="1471490">eigenvalue</span> <span m="1472830">for</span> <span m="1473370">Cayley</span>
  <span m="1473670">graphs.</span> <span m="1473940">And</span> <span m="1474060">what</span>
  <span m="1474210">is</span> <span m="1474330">a</span> <span m="1474390">special

  <span m="1476130">to</span> <span m="1476220">do</span> <span m="1476370">this,</span>

  <span m="1487330">So</span> <span m="1487450">let</span> <span m="1487570">me</span>
  <span m="1487690">define--</span> <span m="1489430">so</span> <span m="1489550">let</span>
  <span m="1489640">me</span> <span m="1489760">first</span> <span m="1490000">tell</span>

  <span m="1493290">So</span> <span m="1493330">this</span> <span m="1493540">is</span>
  <span m="1493650">the</span> <span m="1493690">result</span> <span m="1494830">due</span>
  <span m="1495040">to</span> <span m="1495430">David</span> <span m="1495760">Conlon</span>
  <span m="1496015">and</span> <span m="1496360">myself</span> <span m="1497250">two</span>
  <span m="1497440">years</span> <span m="1497680">ago.</span></p><p><span m="1500570">So</span>
  <span m="1501110">many</span> <span m="1501380">of</span> <span m="1501470">you</span>

  <span m="1510200">by</span> <span m="1510360">the</span> <span m="1510470">initial.</span>
  <span m="1512090">Although</span> <span m="1512270">some</span> <span m="1512480">kind</span>
  <span m="1512720">of</span> <span m="1512780">false</span> <span m="1513170">modesty.</span>
  <span m="1513740">But,</span> <span m="1513890">of</span> <span m="1513980">course,</span>
  <span m="1514370">we</span> <span m="1514490">all</span> <span m="1514610">love</span>
  <span m="1514820">talking</span> <span m="1515120">about</span> <span m="1515270">our</span>
  <span m="1515330">own</span> <span m="1515540">results,</span> <span m="1517280">but</span>
  <span m="1517520">somehow</span> <span m="1517880">we</span> <span m="1518510">don't</span>
  <span m="1518690">like</span> <span m="1518810">to</span> <span m="1518930">write</span>
  <span m="1519140">our</span> <span m="1519260">own</span> <span m="1519410">name</span>
  <span m="1519680">for</span> <span m="1519830">some</span> <span m="1520010">reason.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="1523520">theorem.</span> <span m="1523850">So</span> <span m="1524030">I</span>
  <span m="1524090">start</span> <span m="1524450">with</span> <span m="1524720">a</span>
  <span m="1525050">finite</span> <span m="1525410">group,</span> <span m="1528350">gamma.</span>

  <span m="1531800">S</span> <span m="1532400">of</span> <span m="1532520">gamma</span>
  <span m="1532850">that</span> <span m="1533060">is</span> <span m="1533120">symmetric.</span>
  <span m="1537040">And</span> <span m="1537220">consider</span> <span m="1537510">G</span>
  <span m="1537800">the</span> <span m="1538620">Cayley</span> <span m="1538990">graph.</span>
  <span m="1544220">Let</span> <span m="1544350">me</span> <span m="1544470">right</span>

  <span m="1545730">number</span> <span m="1546090">of</span> <span m="1546390">vertices,</span>
  <span m="1547020">and</span> <span m="1547140">d</span> <span m="1548070">the</span>
  <span m="1548250">size</span> <span m="1548610">of</span> <span m="1548760">S.</span>
  <span m="1549060">So</span> <span m="1549300">this</span> <span m="1549480">is</span>
  <span m="1549600">a</span> <span m="1549690">d</span> <span m="1549930">regular</span>
  <span m="1550920">graph.</span> <span m="1552370">Let</span> <span m="1552490">me</span>
  <span m="1552580">define</span> <span m="1553030">the</span> <span m="1553120">following</span>
  <span m="1553570">properties.</span></p><p><span m="1561550">The</span> <span m="1561650">first</span>
  <span m="1561780">property,</span> <span m="1562590">I'll</span> <span m="1562740">call</span>
  <span m="1563760">DISC</span> <span m="1565020">with</span> <span m="1565200">epsilon.</span>
  <span m="1565680">So</span> <span m="1565830">I</span> <span m="1566370">give</span>
  <span m="1566580">you</span> <span m="1566730">an</span> <span m="1566820">explicit</span>
  <span m="1567330">parameter.</span> <span m="1572290">The</span> <span m="1572530">number</span>
  <span m="1572830">of</span> <span m="1572930">edges</span> <span m="1573280">between</span>
  <span m="1573850">x</span> <span m="1574060">and</span> <span m="1574150">y</span>
  <span m="1574960">differs</span> <span m="1575500">from</span> <span m="1575710">the</span>
  <span m="1575800">number</span> <span m="1576070">of</span> <span m="1576190">edges</span>
  <span m="1577860">that</span> <span m="1578320">you</span> <span m="1578440">would</span>
  <span m="1578560">expect.</span> <span m="1579070">So</span> <span m="1580180">as</span>
  <span m="1580340">in</span> <span m="1580610">the</span> <span m="1580700">expander</span>
  <span m="1581110">mixing</span> <span m="1581410">lemma.</span> <span m="1581980">So</span>
  <span m="1582130">the</span> <span m="1582280">DISC</span> <span m="1582550">property</span>
  <span m="1582930">is</span> <span m="1583130">that</span> <span m="1583270">this</span>
  <span m="1583600">quantity</span> <span m="1584110">is</span> <span m="1584200">small</span>
  <span m="1585010">relative</span> <span m="1585490">to</span> <span m="1585730">the</span>
  <span m="1585880">total</span> <span m="1586210">number</span> <span m="1586510">of</span>
  <span m="1586630">edges.</span></p><p><span m="1590670">The</span> <span m="1590790">second</span>
  <span m="1591090">property,</span> <span m="1591900">which</span> <span m="1592670">we'll</span>
  <span m="1592740">call</span> <span m="1593970">the</span> <span m="1594390">eigenvalue</span>
  <span m="1595170">property,</span> <span m="1595710">EIG,</span> <span m="1596760">is</span>
  <span m="1597000">that</span> <span m="1597750">G</span> <span m="1600191">is</span>
  <span m="1600630">an</span> <span m="1600750">n,</span> <span m="1600990">d,</span>
  <span m="1601140">lambda</span> <span m="1601470">graph,</span> <span m="1606560">with</span>
  <span m="1609410">lambda,</span> <span m="1610110">at</span> <span m="1610250">most,</span>
  <span m="1611210">epsilon</span> <span m="1611780">d.</span> <span m="1612796">So</span>
  <span m="1613230">lambda</span> <span m="1613650">is</span> <span m="1614040">quite</span>
  <span m="1614310">small</span> <span m="1614960">as</span> <span m="1615120">a</span>
  <span m="1615180">function</span> <span m="1615720">of</span> <span m="1615840">d.</span>
  <span m="1619326">The</span> <span m="1619830">conclusion</span> <span m="1620580">of</span>
  <span m="1620700">the</span> <span m="1620790">theorem</span> <span m="1622250">is</span>
  <span m="1622460">that,</span> <span m="1623100">up</span> <span m="1623250">to</span>
  <span m="1623460">a</span> <span m="1624800">small</span> <span m="1625190">change</span>
  <span m="1625520">of</span> <span m="1625580">parameters,</span> <span m="1626340">these</span>
  <span m="1626510">two</span> <span m="1627050">properties</span> <span m="1627560">are</span>
  <span m="1627680">equivalent.</span> <span m="1628790">In</span> <span m="1628880">particular,</span>
  <span m="1630020">eigenvalue</span> <span m="1630590">implies</span> <span m="1632390">a--</span>
  <span m="1633800">epsilon</span> <span m="1634280">implies</span> <span m="1635410">DISC</span>

  <span m="1979070">at most,</span> <span m="1979400">a</span> <span m="1979685">constant</span>
  <span m="1979970">factor.</span> <span m="1982650">So,</span> <span m="1982670">in</span>
  <span m="1982790">other</span> <span m="1982940">words,</span> <span m="1983880">the</span>
  <span m="1983980">left-hand</span> <span m="1984260">side,</span> <span m="1984870">which</span>
  <span m="1984980">is</span> <span m="1985100">known</span> <span m="1985350">as</span>
  <span m="1985490">a</span> <span m="1985610">semi-definite</span> <span m="1986330">relaxation,</span>
  <span m="1995060">you</span> <span m="1995240">are</span> <span m="1995390">not</span>
  <span m="1995690">losing</span> <span m="1996170">by</span> <span m="1996380">more</span>
  <span m="1996590">than</span> <span m="1996770">a</span> <span m="1996800">constant</span>
  <span m="1997280">factor</span> <span m="1997910">compared</span> <span m="1998390">to</span>
  <span m="1998510">the</span> <span m="1998630">original</span> <span m="1999110">problem.</span>
  <span m="2000730">And</span> <span m="2000850">this</span> <span m="2001000">is</span>
  <span m="2001120">important</span> <span m="2001660">in</span> <span m="2001780">computer</span>

  <span m="2002890">left-hand</span> <span m="2003250">side</span> <span m="2003790">turns</span>
  <span m="2004090">out</span> <span m="2004210">to</span> <span m="2004300">be</span>
  <span m="2004510">a</span> <span m="2004660">Semidefinite</span> <span m="2005380">Program,</span>
  <span m="2006070">an</span> <span m="2006340">SDP,</span> <span m="2007690">which</span>
  <span m="2007960">does</span> <span m="2008260">have</span> <span m="2009340">efficient</span>

  <span m="3224300">a</span> <span m="3224390">good</span> <span m="3224600">way</span>

  <span m="4724040">root</span> <span m="4724850">d</span> <span m="4725050">minus
  1</span> <span m="4725300">exactly</span> <span m="4726470">is</span> <span m="4727180">the</span>
  <span m="4727310">spectral</span> <span m="4727700">radius</span> <span m="4733520">of</span>
  <span m="4733790">the</span> <span m="4733940">infinite</span> <span m="4734270">d</span>
  <span m="4734600">regular</span> <span m="4734960">tree.</span> <span m="4738120">And</span>
  <span m="4738600">that</span> <span m="4738750">is</span> <span m="4739260">the</span>
  <span m="4739350">reason,</span> <span m="4739860">in</span> <span m="4739950">some</span>
  <span m="4740130">sense,</span> <span m="4740400">that</span> <span m="4740550">this</span>
  <span m="4740700">is</span> <span m="4740820">the</span> <span m="4740880">correct</span>
  <span m="4741300">number</span> <span m="4742410">occurring</span> <span m="4742940">Alon-Boppana</span>
  <span m="4743490">bound.</span></p><p><span m="4747380">This</span> <span m="4747670">is--</span>
  <span m="4748670">if</span> <span m="4748880">you've</span> <span m="4749360">seen</span>
  <span m="4749960">things</span> <span m="4750230">like</span> <span m="4750440">algebraic</span>
  <span m="4750770">topology</span> <span m="4751310">or</span> <span m="4751400">topology,</span>
  <span m="4751910">this</span> <span m="4752120">is</span> <span m="4752600">a</span>
  <span m="4752855">universal</span> <span m="4753110">cover</span> <span m="4753640">for</span>
  <span m="4754040">d regular</span> <span m="4754400">graphs.</span> <span m="4756040">So</span>
  <span m="4756870">I</span> <span m="4756950">won't</span> <span m="4757130">talk</span>
  <span m="4757370">more</span> <span m="4757520">about</span> <span m="4757700">it,</span>
  <span m="4757820">but</span> <span m="4758710">just</span> <span m="4759050">some</span>
  <span m="4759290">general</span> <span m="4759620">remarks,</span> <span m="4760330">and</span>
  <span m="4760490">you</span> <span m="4760610">already</span> <span m="4760850">saw</span>
  <span m="4761060">two</span> <span m="4761210">different</span> <span m="4761480">proofs.</span>
  <span m="4762310">So</span> <span m="4762500">beginning</span> <span m="4762800">of</span>
  <span m="4762860">next</span> <span m="4763100">time,</span> <span m="4763280">I</span>
  <span m="4763340">want</span> <span m="4763490">to</span> <span m="4763550">wrap</span>
  <span m="4763790">this</span> <span m="4764000">up</span> <span m="4764540">and</span>
  <span m="4764690">to</span> <span m="4764750">show</span> <span m="4765020">you--</span>
  <span m="4765740">to</span> <span m="4765920">explain</span> <span m="4766370">some--</span>
  <span m="4766970">what</span> <span m="4767180">we</span> <span m="4767330">know</span>
  <span m="4767630">about</span> <span m="4768590">are</span> <span m="4768740">there</span>
  <span m="4768920">graphs</span> <span m="4769760">for</span> <span m="4769910">which</span>
  <span m="4770270">this</span> <span m="4770450">bound</span> <span m="4770750">is</span>
  <span m="4770900">tight?</span> <span m="4772540">And</span> <span m="4772660">the</span>
  <span m="4772750">answer</span> <span m="4772990">is</span> <span m="4773110">yes,</span>
  <span m="4773500">and</span> <span m="4773680">there</span> <span m="4773840">are</span>
  <span m="4774080">lots</span> <span m="4774430">of</span> <span m="4774790">major</span>

  <span m="4778330">what</span> <span m="4778480">happens</span> <span m="4778810">there.</span>
  <span m="4779630">And</span> <span m="4779730">then,</span> <span m="4779800">after</span>
